 The case of Cash for Vote in the election is not new, but for the first time in the history of Indian democracy, a Lok Sabha election has been canceled because of getting cash
 kareeb 11 karod rupee cash baraamad hone ke baad tamilnadu ke vellore seat par chunaav radd hua
 President Ram Nath Kovind announced this on Tuesday night on the recommendation of the Election Commission
 chunaav ayog ke is faisle ke baad se siyasat shuru ho gai he
 DM Vellore seat DMK treasurer Duraimurgan's son DM Kathir Anand is the DMK candidate
 chunaav ayog ke is faisle ko duraimurgan ne loktantr kii hatya qaraar diya
 He said that this step has been taken to intimidate the opposition parties
 bataa den, diemke pratyaashee par cash for vot kaa aarope laga he
 It was only after this that the Election Commission recommended the cancellation of the election on 14 April
 kyon radd hua vellore seat par chunaavdarasal, sthaneey prashasan kii shikaayat par iskar vibhaag kii team ne diemke koshadhyaksh durimurgan ke ghar par 30 march ko chhapemari kii
 a day later, on 1 April, a raid was conducted on the cement warehouse of the dmk's party official
 iskar vibhaag ne yahaan se 11 karod rupye kii nagdi baraamad kii
 On 8 April, the Election Commission filed a case against DMK candidate Kathir Anand and his two close associates Poonjolai Srinivasan and Damodaran
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki cement godaam kaa maalik damodaran hi he
 The lawsuit claimed that Poonjolai Srinivasan had admitted that the money belonged to him and was kept in the warehouse to be distributed among the voters
 IPC kii dhaaraon (171 i or 171 bi) or 125 e main kathir anand or punjolai shrinivasana par exiaar darj kiya gaya
 After this, the Election Commission recommended cancellation of the election here on 14 April
 16 april yani mangalvaar kii shaam raashtrapati ramnath kovind ne chunaav ayog kii sifarish par vellore seat kaa chunaav radd kar diya
 Kathir Anand sent notice to Election Commission After the election was canceled, DMK candidate Kathir Anand sent notice to Election Commission
 is notice main kathir ne kaha ki vellore main chunaav karaayaa jaae, nahin to ham kanoonee karrwai karenge
 Kathir wrote that neither any cash was recovered from his house or his mother's house nor any documents, in such a situation, elections should be held
 kathir ne aarope lagaaya ki vellore main chunaav radd karnaa or iskar vibhaag kaa chapa bijepi-annadramuk gathbandhan ke paksh main maahaul banane kii koshish kii tarah lag rahaa he
 Kathir Anand demanded that elections be held for Vellore seat or else legal action will be taken

 2016 main vidhansabha chunaavon ke dauraan, cash for vot ke aarope main thanjavur or aravakurichi ke chunaav radd kar die the

 ) Raghuram Rajan, former Governor of Reserve Bank of India has expressed the possibility of serious threat to capitalism
 unhone kaha ki aarthik or raajnneetik vyavastha main logon ko baraabar avasar uplabdh nahin hue hai
 Because of this, rebellion can arise against capitalism
 ek kaarykram ke dauraan antarrashtriya mudra kosh (imef) ke purv mukhya arthshaastri rajan ne kaha, 'duniyabar kii sarkarein saamaajik asamanta ko nazarandaaj nahin kar sakati hai
 'I believe that capitalism is in grave danger because many people are not getting opportunities in it and when this happens, rebellion against capitalism arises
 'iske saath hi unhone kaha ki meri samaj se poonjeevaad kamjor pad rahaa he kyonki yah logon ko baraabar avasar nahin de rahaa he
 In fact, the condition of those who are being influenced by capitalism has deteriorated
 rajan ne salaah dete hue kaha ki sansadhano kaa santulan jaruri he
 Everyone has the freedom to choose anything they like
 vastav main jarurat is baat kii he ki avasaron kii sthiti main sudhaar ho
 He said that the situation has changed especially after the 2008 economic recession
 purv governor ne udhaaharan dete hue kaha ki pehle maamuli shiksha ke saath madhyam shrenee kii naukari mil jaati thi lekin 2008 ke vaishvik aarthik sankat ke baad sthiti badali he
 If you want to succeed, you really need to get a good education
 vaishvik arthvyavastha kii sthiti ke bare main baat karte hue rajan ne kaha ki agar aap duusare ke vyapaar par pratibandh lagaayenge to wo aapaki vastuon par pratibandh lagaayenge
 He said that the question is, how do you keep your business running across the border and get your goods there
 samudri tufaan ko ek pakshi kaa naam mila or wo ban gaya hudahud
 Now the horror of Hudhud has spread to the maritime areas of India
 har koi daraa hua he ki na jane kab samudr kii lehren vikaraal rup dhaaran kar len
 From meteorologists to state governments, Hudhud's high alert has been issued
 khaas baat yah he ki ye chakravaat har ghante prachand rup le rahaa he or hindustan kii hadon kii taraf bad rahaa he
 Now the danger is hovering over the dense population
 dilli sthit mausam vibhaag ke cyclone centre ke diarector em mahapaatr ne kaha, 'hamaari ashanka he ki ye pashchim va uttar-pashchim disha par gati se aage bad rahaa he
 Gradually it will be catastrophic in the next 24 hours
 bengal kii khadi main mandara rahaa hudahud tufaan apni tabaahi kaa trailor dikhaa chukaa he
 The storm of destruction has crossed Andaman and Nicobar
 hudahud ne andaman-nikaabor main kaaphi tabaahi machaai
 The winds were so strong that the trees were uprooted, roads were broken
 iske saath bijli or phone kii vyavastha bhi thap ho gai
 Now this storm is moving rapidly towards west-north, west
 hudahud dehshat isliye ban chukaa he, kyonki jis disha main vinaash kaa yah tufaan bad rahaa he, vahaan ghani aabaadi he
 That is, falling trees, electricity, and communication lines can collapse
 sabase bada khatra, uttari andhra pradesh or dakshini odisha par he
 Danger on 20 lakh population The biggest danger is that Hudhud is directly hitting Visakhapatnam with a population of over 20 lakh in Andhra Pradesh
 sachai yahi he ki 12 oktober ko jab hudahud hindustan main dastak degaa, hawaaon kii raftaar tufaani hogi, tabaahi kii barish hogi, to bijli, sadak, ped sab dhwast ho sakate hai
 On October 12, Andhra Pradesh and Odisha need to be careful for 12 hours
 hindustan main hudahud ne dehshat kii taarikh bhi mukarrar kar di he
 On October 12, when the clock strikes five and a half in the morning, the sea area will rise
 bhavishyavaanee kuch aisi he
 According to the Meteorological Department, the cyclonic storm Hudhud which is hovering in the Bay of Bengal has shifted towards Andhra Pradesh Visakhapatnam
 12 oktober ko hudahud vishakhapattanam se takaraayega
 Hudhud would then enter the boundaries of Srikakulam via West Godavari, East Godavari, Visakhapatnam and Vizianagaram in Andhra Pradesh
 yahaan 24 se 25 centimetre yani bhayanak barish ho sakati he
 Along with this, one can leave havoc in Ganjam, Gajapati, Koraput and Malkangiri in southern Odisha
 uttari andhra pradesh or odisha main hudahud kii dehshat se rajya sarkarein bhi alert ho chuki hai
 Camps are being set up in Visakhapatnam to avoid the destruction of Hudhud
 odisha ke mukhyamantri kisi bhi aapadaa se nipatane ke liye baithken kar rahe hai
 Winds will be 120 to 130 kilometers per hour inside the sea storm
 ham aapako bataa den ki 11 taarikh ke aate hi hudahud or bhi taqatvar ho jayega
 Within this, the speed of winds will increase from 130 to 140 kilometers per hour
 yah kabhi-kabhi 155 kilometre prati ghanta kii raftaar ko bhi chhu sakati he
 The panic storm is currently 500 km from Visakhapatnam, but warnings have been issued in all districts of southern Odisha, ranging from northern Andhra Pradesh
 odisha ke ganjam jile ke binachapalli main hudahud se bachane ke liye taiyaariyaan chal rahi hai
 Mock drill is being done, so that the fear of Hudhud ends
 logon ko sikhaaya ja rahaa he ki kaise chakravaati tufaan se bachanaa he, lite jane par kya karnaa he, tabaahi se logon ko kaise bachaana he
 Panic now in the name of a bird! Hudhud has become the name of panic and destruction
 hindustan main har koi hudahud ke naam se bhi kaanp rahaa he, lekin jaaniye ki chakravaati tufaan kaa naam hudahud kyon padaa
 The name Hudhud is given by Oman
 ye arabi shabd he
 Hudhud is a bird, which is mentioned in the sacred scriptures there
 yah isroyal kaa rashtriya pakshi bhi he
 Now also know the reason behind the name
 vishwa mausam sanghathan or united neshans iconomic and soshal kamishan for asia and pacific ke jariye jari kii jane vaali prakriyaaon ke tahat kisi bhi chakravaat kaa naam rakhaa jaataa he
 Eight northern Indian maritime countries decide 64 names of cyclones coming together, each of which has eight names
 jaise hi chakravaat in aath deshon ke kisi hisse main pahunchataa he, suchi se aglaa doosraa sulabh naam is chakravaat kaa rakh diya jaataa he
 This process helps in easy identification and rescue operations of the storm
 ye aath desh hai- bangladesh, bharat, maldive, myanmar, oman, pakistan, srilanka or thailand

 patiala ke tohda gaanv ke senior secondary skool main 10veen kaksha kii dalit chaatra ne anusuchit jati ayog ko ek patr likhakar apane saath hue atyaachaar kii aapbeetee bataai he
 Dalit student Veerpal Kaur has said in her complaint that in March 2017, she was asked by the school clerk to copy her nephew and two classmates in the 10th grade examination
 usne nakal nahin karwaai to teenon ladke fail ho gaye
 After the result came in June last year, the three boys ran and beat him in front of everyone in school
 iske baad ek farji fasebuk post banaakar use badnaam karne kii koshish kii gai thi
 When Virpal Kaur's father came to know about this incident, he lodged a complaint in Bhadas police station
 iske baad teenon aropiyon ne chaatra se na keval maafee maangi balki police ko yah bhi bataaya tha ki fasebuk post skool ke clerk ke kehane par aplod kii gai thi

 use jaateey tippaniyan karke pareshaan kiya gaya

 iske baavjood virpal cor skool kii medhaavi chaatra bani rahi
